JFly.Ai
01 · What's built

DiningOut Optimizer

Thinks like an editor · Works like a developer · Delivers like a publisher

01
Editor publishes.
Same workflow as today. The content team writes. The editorial calendar runs. None of it changes.
02
The optimizer.
Reads the article. Finds every restaurant. Looks each one up on Google Business for hours, phone, address. Every fact is quote-grounded, if the editorial team didn't write it, the engine drops it.
03
Schema lands in the page head.
JSON-LD (Restaurant + ItemList + FAQPage) injected into the source. Invisible to readers. Loud to AI. Snapshot saved for rollback. Readers see exactly what they saw yesterday.
Every other schema tool reads your page and tags it as one thing. Ours decomposes it into the entities inside, every restaurant, every list, every answer, and writes the markup Google and AI assistants actually parse.

Optimizer Architecture

Layer Lives where Note
Engine (the brain)JFly.Ai EngineAI-powered + API
Plugin (built-in)Your WordPressOne-click automated
Schema in <head>DiningOut.comGoogle AI Optimizer reads it
Snapshot / rollbackYour WP database90 days of restorable state
Bulk optimizerJFly.Ai EngineAutomated
02 · The problem

Great article. No schema. AI walked past it.

A live ChatGTP search. Exact search is DiningOut’s headline.

Recorded 2026-05-28 · ChatGPT
02 · The solution

What AI is begging for.

Six articles run through Google Rich Results.

Rich Results

↓ click any row for the schema

                    "name": "Which NYC bagel shops have multiple locations?",
                    "acceptedAnswer": {
                        "@type": "Answer",
                        "text": "Several shops on this list operate multiple locations: Ess-a-Bagel, Brooklyn Bagel & Coffee Co. (Manhattan and Queens), Apollo Bagels (half-dozen locations), Tompkins Square Bagels, PopUp Bagels, Modern Bread and Bagel, Utopia Bagels (Queens and Midtown), and H&H Bagels all have more than one NYC outpost. Terrace Bagels and Bagel Hole are single-location shops."
                    }
                }
            ]
        }
    ]

High-level findings from a short pass. Full audit covers eight categories.

144,000→<200
Lifetime views combined → Monthly visits today
→ RecommendationEditorial refresh, republish + update the top-20 dead articles + re-promote in newsletter/social.

Finding 02 · AI discovery plateau
27→345

05 · Why now

The window is open. Now is the time.

DiningOut's schema timing is perfectly positioned with Google's 2026 citation rules. The opportunity to become the new authority is right now.

The 2026 numbers

AI Overview penetration
60%+

of Google searches now show an AI Overview. Up from 25% in mid-2024. The default surface, not the edge case.

Schema = citation
2.3×

more often cited when the page has schema markup. The single biggest page-level lever in AI search.

Sources: Ahrefs 2025 · Digital Applied 1,000-AIO study, April 2026

Why now, specifically

Every week you wait
  • ~60 more articles publish without schema, future backfill cost.
  • Eater, Thrillist, Infatuation eventually figure this out. First-mover window shrinks.
  • AI engines re-cite based on their last visit. Late schema = late citations.
If you start this month
  • Denver listicles earn rich-result eligibility in 3–6 weeks.
  • First AI Overview citations land inside 60–90 days as Google re-crawls.
  • By month 12 you're the most machine-readable restaurant authority in 6 cities.
DiningOut becomes the first food publisher with full schema + editorial coverage end-to-end.
